*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ —Å—Ç—ä–ø–∫–∞ —Å–ª–µ–¥ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞ —Å—ä–¥—ä—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≤ –≥–æ–ª—è–º –æ–±–µ–º.
*   –ò—Ç–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —á–µ–∫–ª–∏—Å—Ç–∞ —Å–∏. –°–ª–µ–¥ –∫–∞—Ç–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç–µ –∫–∞–∫–≤–∏ –≥—Ä–µ—à–∫–∏ –¥–æ–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ AI –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏, –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–æ–≤–∏ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –≥–∏ —É–ª–∞–≤—è—Ç–µ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an AI Quality Assurance (QA) Automation Engineer. Your task is to design the logic for a "QA Bot" that audits the output of another AI agent against a predefined quality standard.

CONTEXT: The user will provide a piece of AI-generated content/data and the specific quality criteria it must meet.

YOUR TASK:
Create a "QA Audit Report" for the provided content.

1.  **Define the Quality Scorecard:** Based on the user's criteria, create a detailed scorecard as a Markdown table. The table should have these columns:
    *   **Criterion:** The quality rule (e.g., "Word Count," "Tone of Voice," "Inclusion of Keywords," "Fact-Checking URLs").
    *   **Requirement:** The specific standard (e.g., "Between 300-350 words," "Professional & helpful," "Must include 'AI Automation'").
    *   **Pass/Fail:** Does the content meet the requirement?
    *   **Score:** Assign points for passing (e.g., 10 points per criterion).
2.  **Conduct the Audit:** Analyze the provided content against each criterion in the scorecard and fill in the "Pass/Fail" and "Score" columns.
3.  **Calculate Total Score & Render Verdict:**
    *   Sum the total points and calculate the final score as a percentage.
    *   Based on the score, render one of three verdicts:
        *   **PASS (90-100%):** "This content meets all quality standards and is approved for use."
        *   **REVIEW (60-89%):** "This content is a good draft but requires minor human review. The specific issues are: [List failed criteria]."
        *   **FAIL (<60%):** "This content does not meet quality standards and must be regenerated. It is being escalated for human review."

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure the output as a formal QA report.

**AI-GENERATED CONTENT FOR AUDIT:** [Paste the content you want to check here.]
**QUALITY CRITERIA:**
[List your quality rules in a clear, bulleted format. e.g.,
- Must be under 200 words.
- Must have a positive and encouraging tone.
- Must include the keyword "Operational Efficiency".
- Must not make any specific statistical claims without citing a source.]
```

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**

*   –†–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç—ä—Ç –µ –ø—Ä–µ–ø–æ—Ä—ä–∫–∞. –ö—Ä–∞–π–Ω–æ—Ç–æ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤—Å–µ –æ—â–µ –∏–∑–∏—Å–∫–≤–∞ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä—Å–∫–∞ –ø—Ä–µ—Ü–µ–Ω–∫–∞, –Ω–æ —Å–µ–≥–∞ —Ç—è –µ –ø–æ–¥–∫—Ä–µ–ø–µ–Ω–∞ —Å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a "Strategic Prioritization Engine," a data-driven Chief of Staff for a high-growth tech company. Your task is to take a list of potential projects and objectively rank them using the R.I.C.E. scoring framework.

**R.I.C.E. Framework:**
*   **Reach:** How many people will this impact over a single quarter?
*   **Impact:** How much will this impact each person? (Scale: 3=massive, 2=high, 1=medium, 0.5=low, 0.25=minimal)
*   **Confidence:** How confident are you in your estimates for Reach and Impact? (Scale: 100%, 80%, 50%)
*   **Effort:** How many "person-months" will this take to complete?
*   **RICE Score = (Reach * Impact * Confidence) / Effort**

CONTEXT: The user will provide a list of potential projects or initiatives.

YOUR TASK:
1.  For each project provided by the user, I need you to ask me for the four R.I.C.E. variables (Reach, Impact, Confidence, Effort). Wait for my input for each project.
2.  Once I provide the variables for all projects, calculate the RICE score for each one.
3.  Generate a "Prioritized Roadmap" as a Markdown table. The table should be sorted from the highest RICE score to the lowest.
4.  The table must have the following columns: [Rank], [Project Name], [Reach], [Impact], [Confidence], [Effort], and [RICE Score].
5.  Conclude with a one-sentence "Executive Recommendation" stating which project the team should focus on first.

Let's begin. Please list your projects, and I will ask for the R.I.C.E. variables for each.

**USER'S PROJECTS:** [User provides a list of projects. e.g., 
- "Revamp the user onboarding flow."
- "Launch a new integration with HubSpot."
- "Rewrite the blog content."]
```

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an Internal Communications and Operations expert. My goal is to automate the generation and distribution of routine internal reports to save leadership time and improve team alignment.

CONTEXT: The user will define a recurring communication need, its audience, and the sources of data.

YOUR TASK:
Design an "Automated Comms Workflow" for the specified need.

1.  **Communication Objective:** State the primary goal of this communication in one sentence.
2.  **Data Sources:** List the specific digital sources from which the data will be pulled (e.g., "Jira tickets closed this week," "HubSpot deals created," "Google Analytics traffic data").
3.  **Content Template Design:** Create a detailed Markdown template for the communication. The template should use placeholders `[dynamic_data]` where the automated system will insert information.
    *   **Subject/Title:** A consistent and clear title.
    *   **Section 1: Highlights (The Good News):** A summary of key achievements.
    *   **Section 2: Key Metrics:** A short list of the most important numbers.
    *   **Section 3: Challenges/Blockers:** A section to flag issues.
    *   **Section 4: Focus for Next Week:** The top 1-2 priorities.
4.  **Distribution Logic:**
    *   **Channel:** Recommend the best channel for this communication (e.g., "Email," "Slack Channel," "Notion Page").
    *   **Cadence:** "This communication will be automatically generated and sent every [Day] at [Time]."
5.  **Implementation Notes:** Suggest how this could be implemented using common automation tools (e.g., "This can be built with Zapier: a scheduled trigger runs every Friday, pulls data from Jira/HubSpot, formats it using this template, and posts it to the #updates Slack channel.").

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use a clear, structured Markdown format that serves as a blueprint for implementation.

RECURRING COMMUNICATION NEED: [e.g., "A weekly summary of the product development team's progress for the whole company."]
AUDIENCE: [e.g., "All employees."]
DATA SOURCES: [e.g., "Jira (for completed stories), Confluence (for documentation updates), GitHub (for merged pull requests)."]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–º—É–Ω–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ, –∫–æ—è –µ –∞—É–¥–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è—Ç–∞ –∏ –æ—Ç–∫—ä–¥–µ –∏–¥–≤–∞—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –ø—ä–ª–µ–Ω –ø–ª–∞–Ω –∑–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ —ä–ø–¥–µ–π—Ç–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –í—Ä–µ–º–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –ª–∏–¥–µ—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –µ –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—è—Ç —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –µ–¥–Ω–∞ –æ—Ç –Ω–∞–π-–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–µ–º–∫–∏—Ç–µ, –Ω–æ –≤–∞–∂–Ω–∏ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ ‚Äì –ø–æ–¥–¥—ä—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –µ–∫–∏–ø–∞ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –∏ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω. –¢–æ–≤–∞ –æ—Å–≤–æ–±–æ–∂–¥–∞–≤–∞ —á–∞—Å–æ–≤–µ –∑–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∞ —Å–µ–¥–º–∏—Ü–∞.

### 24. AI –ë—Ä–æ–∫–µ—Ä –∑–∞ API –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∏ –†–∞–±–æ—Ç–Ω–∏ –ü–æ—Ç–æ—Ü–∏

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –î–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–æ "–ø—Ä–µ–≤–æ–¥–∞—á" –º–µ–∂–¥—É –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å —Ü–µ–ª–∏ –∏ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—è —Å–≤—è—Ç –Ω–∞ API –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏—Ç–µ.
*   –ê–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ, –∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–∞–≥–∞ –Ω–∞–π-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∏ –ª–æ–≥–∏—á–Ω–∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–Ω–∏ –ø–æ—Ç–æ—Ü–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –º–æ–≥–∞—Ç –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–∞—Ç —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Ç—è—Ö.
*   –°—ä–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞ —è—Å–Ω–∞ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è –∑–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∞ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è (—Ç—Ä–∏–≥–µ—Ä, –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ, —Ñ–∏–ª—Ç—Ä–∏), –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –≤ –ø–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–æ Zapier –∏–ª–∏ Make.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ë—ä–¥–µ—Ç–µ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ, –∏ –∑–∞ "–±–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—Ç–µ" —Ä—ä—á–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Å—ä—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–≤–∞—Ç –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Ç—è—Ö –≤ –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞.
*   –ó–∞–ø–æ—á–Ω–µ—Ç–µ —Å –Ω–∞–π-–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∞ –∏ –Ω–∞–π-—á–µ—Å—Ç–æ —Å—Ä–µ—â–∞–Ω–∞ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∞. –ï–¥–Ω–∞ –º–∞–ª–∫–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∏ 100 –ø—ä—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –¥–µ–Ω, –µ –ø–æ-—Ü–µ–Ω–Ω–∞ –æ—Ç —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∏ –≤–µ–¥–Ω—ä–∂ –º–µ—Å–µ—á–Ω–æ.
*   –ù–µ —Å–µ –æ–ø–∏—Ç–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–æ. –§–æ–∫—É—Å–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–µ –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É –ø—Ä–µ—Ö–≤—ä—Ä–ª—è–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏ –∏ –Ω–æ—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Å–ø–µ—Å—Ç—è–≤–∞—Ç –Ω–∞–π-–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as an "Integration & Workflow Architect." You have deep knowledge of hundreds of SaaS application APIs and are an expert in designing efficient workflows using platforms like Zapier or Make.com.

CONTEXT: The user will list the key software tools they use and describe a manual process that involves moving data between them.

YOUR TASK:
Analyze the user's tech stack and manual process, then design the top 3 most impactful automation workflows. For each workflow:

1.  **Workflow Name:** Give it a clear, descriptive name (e.g., "New Lead to Sales & Project Management Sync").
2.  **Business Value:** In one sentence, explain how this automation saves time, reduces errors, or accelerates a process.
3.  **The "Zap" Blueprint:** Provide a clear, step-by-step recipe for building the automation.
    *   **Tool 1 (Trigger App):** The application where the process starts.
    *   **The Trigger:** The specific event that kicks off the workflow (e.g., "New Form Submission").
    *   **Filters (Optional):** Any conditions that must be met for the workflow to continue (e.g., "Only continue if 'Budget' field is > $1000").
    *   **Tool 2 (Action App):** The application where the action happens.
    *   **The Action:** The specific event that the workflow performs (e.g., "Create New Deal," "Create Task").
    *   **Data Mapping:** Specify which information from the trigger step maps to which field in the action step.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Structure the response as a list of three "Workflow Recipes."

OUR KEY SOFTWARE TOOLS: [e.g., "Webflow (for our website), HubSpot (for CRM), Slack (for communication), Asana (for project management)."]
MANUAL PROCESS WE HATE: [e.g., "When a new lead fills out the form on our Webflow site, our marketing assistant has to manually copy their information to create a new deal in HubSpot, then create a task in Asana for the sales rep, and then post a notification in our #new-leads Slack channel."]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –ò–∑–±—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ, –∏ –æ–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ —Ä—ä—á–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –µ–ª–∏–º–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ –∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ—Ç–µ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–∏ "—Ä–µ—Ü–µ–ø—Ç–∏", –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ –¥–∞ –≤–Ω–µ–¥—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –≤–µ–¥–Ω–∞–≥–∞.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –°–∏–ª–∞—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –º–æ–¥–µ—Ä–Ω–∏—è –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å –Ω–µ –µ –≤ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏, –∞ –≤ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞, –ø–æ –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ —Ç–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—è—Ç –∑–∞–µ–¥–Ω–æ. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –µ "–ª–µ–ø–∏–ª–æ—Ç–æ". –¢–æ–π –≤–∏ –ø–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–¥–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∏–≥–∏—Ç–∞–ª–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Ä–≤–Ω–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞, –≤ –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ —Ç–µ—á–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –∏ –±–µ–∑–ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–Ω–æ, –µ–ª–∏–º–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞–π–∫–∏ "copy-paste" —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–≤–∏–Ω–∞–≥–∏.

### 25. –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞ –ê–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –û–¥–∏—Ç–Ω–∏ –ü—ä—Ç–µ–∫–∏ (Compliance Bot)

**üéØ –ö–∞–∫–≤–æ –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç (What This Prompt Does):**
*   –ü—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∑–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ –≤–æ–¥–µ–Ω–µ –Ω–∞ "–æ–¥–∏—Ç–Ω–∞ –ø—ä—Ç–µ–∫–∞" (audit trail) –∑–∞ –≤—Å–µ–∫–∏ –≤–∞–∂–µ–Ω, –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å.
*   –î–µ—Ñ–∏–Ω–∏—Ä–∞ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ –∫–∞–∫–≤–∞ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–≤–∞ (–ª–æ–≥–≤–∞) –Ω–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∞ —Å—Ç—ä–ø–∫–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ —Å–µ –æ—Å–∏–≥—É—Ä–∏ –ø—ä–ª–Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–æ—Å—Ç –∏ –≤—ä–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç –∑–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞.
*   –ü–æ–º–∞–≥–∞ –≤–∏ –¥–∞ –¥–æ–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç–µ —Å—ä–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ —Å —Ä–µ–≥—É–ª–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (compliance) –∏ –¥–∞ –¥–∏–∞–≥–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∏ –≤ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∏, –∫–∞—Ç–æ —Å—ä–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞ –Ω–µ–∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–º –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å –∑–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–æ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ, –∏–∑–≤—ä—Ä—à–µ–Ω–æ –æ—Ç AI.

**üí° –°—ä–≤–µ—Ç–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∞–π-–¥–æ–±—Ä–∏ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ (Tips):**
*   –ò–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –∑–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å–∏, –∫–æ–∏—Ç–æ —Å–∞ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤–æ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª–Ω–∏, –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–≤–∞—Ç –ª–∏—á–Ω–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏ (GDPR) –∏–ª–∏ —Å–∞ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏ –∑–∞ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏—Ç–µ.
*   –õ–æ–≥–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –±—ä–¥–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ. –í—Å—è–∫–æ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –Ω–∞ AI —Ç—Ä—è–±–≤–∞ –¥–∞ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–∞ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å –≤ —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –ª–æ–≥ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä. Google Sheet –∏–ª–∏ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª–Ω–∞ –±–∞–∑–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–∏).
*   –†–µ–¥–æ–≤–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–≥–ª–µ–∂–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ –ª–æ–≥ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–æ–≤–µ—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –∞–Ω–æ–º–∞–ª–∏–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –ø–æ–≤—Ç–∞—Ä—è—â–∏ —Å–µ –≥—Ä–µ—à–∫–∏.

**üíª THE GOD PROMPT (English):**
```text
Act as a "Compliance & Systems Audit Specialist." Your task is to design an automated audit trail (logging system) for a critical, automated business process to ensure transparency, accountability, and regulatory compliance.

CONTEXT: The user will describe a sensitive, automated workflow.

YOUR TASK:
Design an "Automated Audit Trail Specification."

1.  **Define Loggable Events:** Analyze the workflow and identify every critical event that must be logged. An event is typically a state change (e.g., "record created," "status changed," "approval given").
2.  **Design the Log Schema:** Create a specification for the "master log" database (e.g., a Google Sheet or a database table). Define the essential columns (fields) that each log entry must contain.
    *   **Timestamp:** (ISO 8601 format) - When the event happened.
    *   **Process ID:** A unique identifier for the overall workflow instance.
    *   **Event Name:** A clear, human-readable name for the event.
    *   **Actor:** Who or what performed the action (e.g., "AI Agent Alpha," "Human: [User ID]").
    *   **Status:** (e.g., "Success," "Failure," "Pending Approval").
    *   **Key Data:** A JSON field containing the most important data associated with the event (e.g., `{"customer_id": "123", "amount": "500"}`).
    *   **Error Message (if applicable):** The specific error if the status is "Failure."
3.  **Implementation Logic:**
    *   For each step in the user's workflow, specify exactly when the log entry should be created (e.g., "Immediately *after* the Stripe payment is successfully processed, create a log entry...").
4.  **Reporting & Alerting:**
    *   Suggest one simple automated report to be generated from the logs (e.g., "A daily summary of all failed transactions.").
    *   Propose one critical alert (e.g., "If the same Process ID fails more than 3 times in an hour, send an immediate alert to the engineering team.").

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Use a structured, technical brief format in Markdown.

SENSITIVE AUTOMATED WORKFLOW: [Describe the critical process. e.g., "An automated process that approves expense reports under $200. It checks the employee's department budget, verifies the receipt with OCR, and triggers a payment via our bank's API."]
```
üìù **–ö–∞–∫ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–ø–æ–ª–∑–≤–∞—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç–∞ (How to Use):**
1.  **–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ:** –ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ü–µ–ª–∏—è –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.
2.  **–ü–æ–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –û–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç–µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏–∑–∏—Ä–∞–Ω –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å, –∫–æ–π—Ç–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–µ–Ω –∏ —Å–∏–≥—É—Ä–µ–Ω.
3.  **–ò–∑–ø—ä–ª–Ω–µ—Ç–µ:** –°—Ç–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π—Ç–µ –≥–æ, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è—Ç–∞ –∑–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞, –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ 100% –≤–∏–¥–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç –∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª –≤—ä—Ä—Ö—É –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ AI –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏.

üöÄ **–ó–∞—â–æ –≤–∏ –µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω (Context):** –° –Ω–∞—Ä–∞—Å—Ç–≤–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–º–∏—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ AI, –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ—Ç–æ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞—Ç –∞–±—Å–æ–ª—é—Ç–Ω–æ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–∏. –¢–æ–∑–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç –≤–∏ –¥–∞–≤–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ç–∞, –∑–∞ –¥–∞ –∏–∑–≥—Ä–∞–¥–∏—Ç–µ —Ç–æ–≤–∞ –¥–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–µ. –¢–æ–π –µ –≤–∞—à–∞—Ç–∞ "—á–µ—Ä–Ω–∞ –∫—É—Ç–∏—è", –∫–æ—è—Ç–æ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–≤–∞ –≤—Å–∏—á–∫–æ, –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–∞–π–∫–∏, —á–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –¥–∞ –æ—Ç–≥–æ–≤–∞—Ä—è—Ç–µ –∑–∞ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ç–µ AI –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥ —Ä–µ–≥—É–ª–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏, –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∏ –∏ —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–∏ –µ–∫–∏–ø.
